[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702549234219/Snipaste_2023-12-14_17-07-02.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702549234219/Snipaste_2023-12-14_17-07-02.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702549245917/Snipaste_2023-12-14_17-05-10.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702549245917/Snipaste_2023-12-14_17-05-10.png)

6、  开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【设置-风扇】，打开打印头两侧的鼓风风扇，观察到两侧鼓风风扇正常旋转后，重新调平打印头就可以正常使用

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702550008915/111%281%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702550008915/111%281%29.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702550016530/222%281%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141051mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702550016530/222%281%29.png)


# 更换喷嘴

## 需要的工具和材料

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 5.0mm十字螺丝刀

● 喷嘴

● M6套筒扳手/6mm六角扳手

● 钳子

● 镊子

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702369530798/image.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702369530798/image.jpg)

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

在执行这些操作时，请采取所有必要的预防措施，建议佩戴隔热手套。对于某些操作，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却再作业。

## 操作步骤

## 1-拆开打印头前盖和左右风扇支架

1、  操作前需先抽出耗材，然后关闭打印机电源，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370066242/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370066242/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370102343/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370102343/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370118264/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370118264/image.png)

2、  分离打印头整体组件的前盖，拔掉"挤出转接板"中"接近开关"的连接线端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370150785/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370150785/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370169110/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370169110/image.png)

3、  使用十字螺丝刀拧松"风扇支架"的四颗固定螺丝（左右各两颗），  取掉"风扇支架"组件，并放到打印头组件顶部（梳理好排线后，更容易摆放）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370189620/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370189620/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370209659/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370209659/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370297230/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370297230/image.png)

## 2-更换喷嘴

1、  取掉加热块上包裹的黑色"硅胶套"（确保喷嘴已经完全冷却）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608045571/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-38-45.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608045571/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-38-45.png)

2、  开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【准备-温度】，然后在温度控制界面，将喷嘴温度设置加热到200℃

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608060341/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-39-34.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608060341/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-39-34.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608073161/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-40-18.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608073161/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-40-18.png)

3、  使用钳子夹着方形金属加热块，然后使用6mm套筒扳手或者6mm的开口扳手拧松喷嘴并取出（在喷嘴加热的情况下进行操作），换上新的喷嘴

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370490788/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370490788/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370504153/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370504153/image.png)

4、关闭打印机，等待喷嘴完全冷却，安装加热块上包裹的黑色"硅胶套"

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370556905/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370556905/image.png)

## 3-装回风扇支架和打印头前盖

1、  将"风扇支架"组件放到安装位置（对准两侧螺丝孔位置更容易安装），使用十字螺丝刀拧紧"风扇支架"的四颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370189620/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702370189620/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371030764/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371030764/image.png)

2、  使用镊子夹着"接近开关"的连接线，将其插入"挤出转接板"的端口中

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371829358/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371829358/image.png)

3、  安装打印头整体组件的前盖（有凹槽设计，滑入方式安装），使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371864029/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371864029/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371900510/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725141259mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702371900510/image.png)

4、  在触摸屏上重新调平后即可正常使用


# 更换喉内铁弗龙管
## 需要的工具和材料

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 尖嘴钳

● PTFE管

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359285076/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359285076/image.png)

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作中的一些涉及高温打印头的操作具有一定危险性。在执行这些操作时，请采取所有必要的预防措施，建议佩戴隔热手套。对于某些操作，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却再作业。

## 操作步骤

## 1-拆下打印头

1、  关闭打印机电源，拔掉位于打印头正后方的风扇组件的端口线，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松"后风扇组件"的三颗固定螺丝，取下后风扇组件

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359374426/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359374426/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359400925/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359400925/image.png)

2、  使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359431521/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359431521/image.png)

3、  使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝，并取下打印头整体组件

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359455917/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359455917/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359476745/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359476745/image.png)

## 2-更换喉管内PTFE管

1、  分离打印头整体组件的前盖，使用十字螺丝刀拧松"风扇支架"的四颗固定螺丝（左右各两颗）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608712149/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-48-41.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702608712149/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-48-41.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719193328833/image%20%282%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719193328833/image%20%282%29.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359605252/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359605252/image.png)

2、  拔掉挤出转接板中"接近开关"的连接线端口，向下取掉"风扇支架"组件放到喷嘴后方

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719193529441/3%20%282%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719193529441/3%20%282%29.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719193554824/4%20%282%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719193554824/4%20%282%29.png)

3、  使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"连接件"的一颗螺丝，并取掉连接件，拔掉挤出转接板中"加热管"的连接线端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359717636/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359717636/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359737252/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359737252/image.png)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"喷嘴组件"的两颗固定螺丝，向下取出"喷嘴组件"

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609064081/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-55-52.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609064081/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-55-52.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609074382/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-56-48.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609074382/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-56-48.png)

5、  将加热棒的线端口插入挤出转接板的"HE0"端口，并将打印头整体平放在打印平台表面（需加热喷嘴，避免喷嘴与打印平台直接接触）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359827763/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359827763/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359848150/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359848150/image.png)

6、  开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【准备-温度】，然后在温度控制界面，将喷嘴温度加热到220℃

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359888767/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359888767/image.png)

7、  在喷嘴高温的情况下，使用钳子夹着打印头组件的散热快，然后拔出喉管内的铁氟龙管。（注意高温，喷嘴和加热块不能触碰）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359960249/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702359960249/image.png)

8、取出新的"铁氟龙管"，并插入喉管内（向下按压，确保插到喉管最底部）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360093633/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360093633/image.png)

9、  关闭打印机电源，拔掉挤出转接板中"加热棒"的连接线端口，然后将"喷嘴组件"放到安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609267712/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-59-38.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609267712/Snipaste_2023-12-15_10-59-38.png)

10、  将加热棒的线端口插入挤出转接板的"HE0"端口，取出"连接件"，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧一颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360158196/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360158196/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609291061/Snipaste_2023-12-15_11-00-44.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702609291061/Snipaste_2023-12-15_11-00-44.png)

11、  将"风扇支架"组件对准两侧螺丝孔进行安装，然后将"接近开关"的连接线插入到"挤出转接板"中的PS端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360207747/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360207747/image.png)

12、  安装打印头整体组件的前盖（有凹槽设计，滑入方式安装）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360233170/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360233170/image.png)

## 3-安装打印头

1、  将打印头整体组件放到打印头前方安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360259148/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702360259148/image.png)

2、  使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719194091236/5%20%282%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719194091236/5%20%282%29.png)

3、  取出风扇组件，对准螺丝孔安装位置，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧后风扇组件的三颗固定螺丝（出风口朝下安装），插入风扇组件接口线端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719194104265/6%20%282%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719194104265/6%20%282%29.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719194005278/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714115041mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1719194005278/image.png)

4、  开启打印机电源，重新调平后就可以正常使用


# 更换加热棒和热敏电阻
 2024-05-11 177

Neptune 4&4Pro 更换加热棒和热敏电阻

## 需要的工具和材料

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 1.5mm内六角扳手

● 十字螺丝刀

● 加热管

● 热敏电阻

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348169536/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348169536/image.png)

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作涉及一些打印头组件的更换，在执行这些操作前，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却再作业。

## 操作步骤

## 1-拆下打印头

1、关闭打印机电源，拔掉位于打印头正后方的风扇组件的端口线，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松"后风扇组件"的三颗固定螺丝，取下后风扇组件

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348995566/image1%E5%89%AF%E6%9C%AC.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348995566/image1%E5%89%AF%E6%9C%AC.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348370507/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348370507/image.png)

2、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348459565/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702348459565/image.png)

3、  用手向两侧按压"牛角端子"，打印头排线会自动弹出，然后取出打印头排线

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349191267/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349191267/image.png)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝，并取下打印头整体组件

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349208020/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349208020/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349221162/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349221162/image.png)

## 2-更换加热管与热敏电阻

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349378777/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349378777/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349443194/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349443194/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349331405/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349331405/image.png)

2、  拔掉挤出转接板中"接近开关"的连接线端口，向下取掉"风扇支架"组件

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349485374/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349485374/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349495078/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349495078/image.png)

3、  取下包裹加热块的黑色"硅胶套"，拔掉挤出转接板中加热管连接线的端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349537810/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349537810/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349703801/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349703801/image.png)

4、  使用1.5mm内六角扳手拧松固定"加热管"的一颗螺丝，并取下加热管（可以仅拧松螺丝而不拿掉）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349738535/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349738535/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349645854/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349645854/image.png)

5、将新的加热管插入到加热管安装孔内（加热管两端需要与加热块表面平齐，不能有过多超出），使用1.5mm内六角扳手将固定加热管的螺丝拧紧

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349790607/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349790607/image.png)

6、将加热管的线端口插入转接板的"HE0"端口（端口有防呆设计，注意区分）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349825481/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349825481/image.png)

7、  拔掉挤出转接板中"热敏电阻"连接线的端口，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"热敏电阻"的一颗固定螺丝，并取下热敏电阻

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349874985/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349874985/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349892258/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349892258/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349907200/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349907200/image.png)

8、取出新的"热敏电阻"，并将其插入到热敏电阻安装孔内，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧固定"热敏电阻"的一颗螺丝 

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349948447/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702349948447/image.png)

9.将热敏电阻的线端口插入挤出转接板的"TH1"端口（端口有防呆设计，注意区分），安装包裹加热块的黑色"硅胶套"

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351318434/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351318434/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351362076/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351362076/image.png)

## 3-安装打印头

1、  将"风扇支架"组件对准两侧螺丝孔进行安装，然后将"接近开关"的连接线插入到"挤出转接板"中的PS端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351454501/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351454501/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351477034/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351477034/image.png)

2、安装打印头整体组件的前盖（有凹槽设计，滑入方式安装）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351521386/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351521386/image.png)

3、将打印头整体组件放到打印头前方安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351558014/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351558014/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351570912/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351570912/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351585823/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351585823/image.png)

4、  用手向两侧按压"牛角自锁端子"打开端口，然后将打印头排线端口插入端口（注意排线从顶部型材下方穿过）

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351606596/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351606596/image.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351652116/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351652116/image.png)

5、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351687098/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351687098/image.png)

6、  取出风扇组件，对准螺丝孔安装位置，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧后风扇组件的三颗固定螺丝（出风口朝下安装），插入风扇组件接口线端口

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351720614/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351720614/image.png)

7、  开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【准备-温度】，然后在温度控制界面点击"PLA"，打印机会开始加入喷嘴和热床，观察到加热温度一切正常后，重新调平后就可以正常使用

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351774551/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714105740mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1702351774551/image.png)


# 调节Y轴偏心轮
## 需要调节偏心轮的情况

● 热床滑行状态异常，明显晃动，需调节Y轴滑台组件的偏心轮。

## 需要的工具

● 随机配套的轮子调节扳手

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699939754590/%E6%8B%BC%E5%9B%BE01.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699939754590/%E6%8B%BC%E5%9B%BE01.png)

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作中需拆热床，在执行这些操作之前，需采取所有必要的预防措施，请关闭机器并等待热床完全冷却。

## 操作步骤

1、 拧松四个调平旋钮， 将热床整体拿到机器后方放置，并取下四颗调平弹簧。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942537554/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942537554/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941759862/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941759862/2.png)

2、拧松Y轴皮带张紧器的旋钮，并从打印平台支架上取下Y轴皮带的前端。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941827675/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941827675/3.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941839223/4.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941839223/4.png)

3、使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松打印平台支架的四颗固定螺丝，将打印平台支架拿到机器后方放置。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941867639/5.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941867639/5.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942129817/6.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942129817/6.png)

4、检查Y轴滑台组件有明显晃动，用专用的轮子调节扳手，拧紧两个偏心轮（两个偏心轮需要同步调节），将偏心轮调节到不会随意晃动，顺畅运行，不会过松或者过紧即可。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941909279/7.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699941909279/7.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942157396/8.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942157396/8.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942169592/9.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942169592/9.png)

5、将打印平台支架放到安装位置，对准螺丝孔，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧打印平台支架的四颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942284010/5.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942284010/5.png)

6、将皮带后方挂在Y轴电机齿轮上，然后将前方的皮带前端卡入打印平台支架的皮带凹槽呢内。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942317243/10.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942317243/10.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942324907/11.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942324907/11.png)

7、转动Y轴皮带张紧器的旋钮，调节到皮带张力适中，不会过松或过紧即可。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942624670/16.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942624670/16.png)

8、将四颗调平弹簧放置到安装位置，把热床整体放置到弹簧上方，并且将四颗调平螺丝插入到四颗弹簧中，拧紧四颗调平旋钮。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942606691/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725135028mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699942606691/1.png)

9、开机，重新手动调平和自动调平打印机后就可以正常使用。

# 调节X轴偏心轮
## 需要调节偏心轮的情况

● 工具头滑行状态异常，明显晃动，需调节X轴滑台组件的偏心轮。

## 需要的工具

● 随机配套的轮子调节扳手

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699939754590/%E6%8B%BC%E5%9B%BE01.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699939754590/%E6%8B%BC%E5%9B%BE01.png)

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作中需拆卸工具头，在执行这些操作之前，需采取所有必要的预防措施，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却。

## 操作步骤

### 1-拆下打印头

1、关闭打印机电源，拔掉位于打印头正后方的风扇组件的端口线，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松"后风扇组件"的三颗固定螺丝，取下后风扇组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005214577/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005214577/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005221869/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005221869/2.png)

2、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005408080/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005408080/3.png)

3、用手向两侧按压"牛角端子"，打印头排线会自动弹出，然后取出打印头排线。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005438771/IMG_9261.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005438771/IMG_9261.jpg)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝，并取下打印头整体组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005459502/5.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005459502/5.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005468788/6.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005468788/6.png)

5、检查X轴滑台组件有明显晃动，用专用的轮子调节扳手，拧紧偏心轮，将偏心轮调节到不会随意晃动，顺畅运行，不会过松或者过紧即可。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699940168068/6.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699940168068/6.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699940183312/7.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699940183312/7.png)

6、将打印头整体组件放到打印头前方安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240997226/24.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240997226/24.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241006164/25.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241006164/25.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241014609/26.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241014609/26.png)

7、用手向两侧按压"牛角自锁端子"打开端口，然后将打印头排线端口插入端口（注意排线从顶部型材下方穿过）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241069003/IMG_9261.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241069003/IMG_9261.jpg)

8、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241124291/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241124291/3.png)

9、取出风扇组件，对准螺丝孔安装位置，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧后风扇组件的三颗固定螺丝（出风口朝下安装），插入风扇组件接口线端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241190027/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241190027/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241197359/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241197359/2.png)

10、开启打印机电源，重新调平后就可以正常使用。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241226923/29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725123709mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241226923/29.png)
# 更换喷嘴组件
## 需要的工具和材料

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 5.0mm十字螺丝刀

● 喷嘴组件

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作涉及对打印头组件的更换，在执行这些操作前，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却再作业。

## 操作步骤

### 1-拆下打印头

1、关闭打印机电源，拔掉位于打印头正后方的风扇组件的端口线，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松"后风扇组件"的三颗固定螺丝，取下后风扇组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005214577/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005214577/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005221869/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005221869/2.png)

2、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005408080/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005408080/3.png)

3、用手向两侧按压"牛角端子"，打印头排线会自动弹出，然后取出打印头排线。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005438771/IMG_9261.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005438771/IMG_9261.jpg)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝，并取下打印头整体组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005459502/5.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005459502/5.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005468788/6.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005468788/6.png)

### 2-更换喷嘴组件

1、分离打印头整体组件的前盖，使用十字螺丝刀拧松"风扇支架"的四颗固定螺丝（左右各两颗）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005495504/7.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005495504/7.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005852616/8.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005852616/8.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005860562/9.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699005860562/9.png)

2、拔掉挤出转接板中"接近开关"的连接线端口，向下取掉"风扇支架"组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237110952/10.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237110952/10.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237121363/11.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237121363/11.png)

3、拔掉挤出转接板中"加热棒"和"热敏电阻"连接线的端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237140285/12.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237140285/12.png)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"连接件"的一颗螺丝，并取掉连接件，再拧松"喷嘴组件"的两颗固定螺丝，取掉"喷嘴组件"和"铁氟龙管"。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237161190/13.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237161190/13.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237167779/14.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237167779/14.png)

5、取出新的"喷嘴组件"（需要重新插入铁氟龙管，确保插到喉管最底部），放到安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"喷嘴组件"的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237186994/15.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237186994/15.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237194774/16.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237194774/16.png)

6、取出"连接件",使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧一颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237220428/17.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237220428/17.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237233939/18.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237233939/18.png)

7、将加热棒的线端口插入挤出转接板的"HE0"端口，将热敏电阻的线端口插入挤出转接板的"TH1"端口（端口有防呆设计，注意区分）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237303846/19.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237303846/19.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237311204/20.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699237311204/20.png)

### 3-安装打印头

1、 将"风扇支架"组件对准两侧螺丝孔进行安装，然后将"接近开关"的连接线插入到"挤出转接板"中的PS端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240928314/21.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240928314/21.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240935219/22.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240935219/22.png)

2、安装打印头整体组件的前盖（有凹槽设计，滑入方式安装）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240962707/23.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240962707/23.png)

3、将打印头整体组件放到打印头前方安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240997226/24.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699240997226/24.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241006164/25.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241006164/25.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241014609/26.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241014609/26.png)

4、用手向两侧按压"牛角自锁端子"打开端口，然后将打印头排线端口插入端口（注意排线从顶部型材下方穿过）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241069003/IMG_9261.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241069003/IMG_9261.jpg)

5、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头的两颗固定螺丝

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241124291/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241124291/3.png)

6、取出风扇组件，对准螺丝孔安装位置，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧后风扇组件的三颗固定螺丝（出风口朝下安装），插入风扇组件接口线端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241190027/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241190027/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241197359/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124742mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1699241197359/2.png)

7、开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【准备-温度】，然后在温度控制界面点击"PLA"，打印机会开始加入喷嘴和热床，观察到加热温度一切正常后，重新调平后就可以正常使用。

# 清理喷嘴漏料
## 引起喷嘴漏料的因素

● 喷嘴堵塞：最常见的原因之一是喷嘴内部堵塞，这可能是由于材料残留或颗粒堵塞喷嘴孔道引起的，使用劣质耗材也可能导致喷嘴堵塞。堵塞会导致材料在不适当的时候流出，从而引发漏料问题。

● 温度设置不当：3D打印需要精确的温度控制，包括喷嘴温度和加热床温度。如果温度设置不正确，材料可能会不正常地流动，导致漏料问题。

● 喷嘴磨损：随着时间的推移，3D打印机的喷嘴可能会磨损，喷嘴孔道变得不均匀，这可能导致材料不稳定地流出，引发漏料问题。

● 打印速度设置不当：过高的打印速度可能会导致喷嘴无法跟上材料的流动，从而引发漏料。

● 打印机维护不当：不定期的维护，如清洗喷嘴、更换损坏的部件等，对于预防漏料问题非常重要。

## 如何确认喷嘴漏料

1.  根据实际使用的材料，加热喷嘴到合适的打印温度。

2.  手动将耗材插入挤出机内，点击屏幕上的进料图标，操作进料50mm。

3.  打印头上的齿轮转动，喷嘴如果没有出料或者出料流量少，可能喷嘴出现了堵塞。

4.  检查喷嘴周围是否有材料积聚，特别是在打印开始之前或停止时。这可能是由于漏料导致的。

## 需要的工具

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

● 5.0mm十字螺丝刀

● 斜口钳

● 镊子

● M6套筒扳手

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作中的一些涉及高温打印头的操作具有一定危险性。在执行这些操作时，请采取所有必要的预防措施，建议佩戴隔热手套。对于某些操作，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却再作业。

## 操作步骤

### 1-拆下打印头

1、关闭打印机电源，拔掉位于打印头正后方的风扇组件的端口线，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松"后风扇组件"的三颗固定螺丝，取下后风扇组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698976934158/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698976934158/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698976943084/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698976943084/2.png)

2、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982133734/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982133734/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982141945/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982141945/2.png)

3、最后拧松"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝，并取下打印头整体组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982163229/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982163229/3.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982170368/4.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982170368/4.png)

### 2-清理喷嘴漏料

1、开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【准备-温度】，在温度控制界面，将喷嘴温度设置加热到220℃。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982207339/5.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982207339/5.png)

2、使用斜口钳清理喷嘴周围漏出来的耗材（如果清理困难，可以适当提高喷嘴温度或者使用热风枪吹风辅助加热，耗材变软后更容易清理）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982239342/6.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982239342/6.png)

3、清理掉大块残留物后，使用镊子夹着纸巾擦拭加热块和喷嘴表面（操作时建议佩戴防护用具，以免烫伤）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982264350/7.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982264350/7.png)

4、使用十字螺丝刀拧松"风扇支架"的四颗固定螺丝，左右各两颗（如果残留物不多，没有干涉到外壳，可以将此步骤提前操作）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982287781/8.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982287781/8.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982296289/9.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982296289/9.png)

5、拔掉"挤出转接板"中"接近开关"的连接线端口，向下取出"喷嘴组件"，将其放到喷嘴后方，接着将余料清理干净。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982321585/10.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982321585/10.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982327995/11.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982327995/11.png)

### 3-安装打印头

1、  将"风扇支架"组件对准两侧螺丝孔进行安装，然后将"接近开关"的连接线插入到"挤出转接板"中 的PS端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982863183/%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E5%BE%AE%E4%BF%A1%E6%88%AA%E5%9B%BE_16989827718218%281%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982863183/%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E5%BE%AE%E4%BF%A1%E6%88%AA%E5%9B%BE_16989827718218%281%29.png)

2、使用十字螺丝刀拧紧"风扇支架"的四颗固定螺丝，用钳子夹着方形金属加热块，然后用M6套筒扳手或者M6的开口扳手拧紧喷嘴，预防继续漏出耗材（在喷嘴加热的情况下进行操作）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982373718/13.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982373718/13.png)

3、安装打印头整体组件的前盖（有凹槽设计，滑入方式安装）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982400559/14.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982400559/14.png)

5、关闭打印机电源，等待喷嘴完全冷却，再安装加热块上的包裹喷嘴的黑色"硅胶套"。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982424022/15.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982424022/15.png)

5、将打印头整体组件放到打印头前方安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982443995/16.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982443995/16.png)

6、使用2.0内六角扳手拧紧"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，和打印头的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982469932/17.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982469932/17.png)

7、取出风扇组件，对准螺丝孔安装位置，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧后风扇组件的三颗固定螺丝（出风口朝下安装），插入风扇组件接口线端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982626598/18.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982626598/18.png)

8、开启打印机电源，重新调平打印机后就可以正常使用。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982505623/19.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725124600mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698982505623/19.png)

# 更换模型散热风扇
 2024-06-24 189

Neptune 4&4pro 更换模型散热风扇

## 需要的工具

● 2.5mm内六角扳手

● 2.0mm内六角扳手

● 十字螺丝刀

## 参考视频

## 操作前的注意事项及机器状态

本次操作涉及对一些打印头组件的更换，在执行这些操作前，请关闭机器并等待打印头完全冷却再作业。

## 操作步骤

### 1-拆下打印头

1、 关闭打印机电源，拔掉位于打印头正后方的风扇组件的端口线，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧松"后风扇组件"的三颗固定螺丝，并取下后风扇组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745094153/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745094153/1.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745109719/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745109719/2.png)

2、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头整体组件的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745124458/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745124458/3.png)

3、  用手向两侧按压"牛角端子"，打印头排线会自动弹出，然后取出打印头排线。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745141597/IMG_9261.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745141597/IMG_9261.jpg)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝，并取下打印头整体组件。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745163026/5.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745163026/5.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745177923/6.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745177923/6.png)

### 2-更换模型散热风扇

1、分离打印头整体组件的前盖，使用十字螺丝刀拧松"导风罩"底部的五颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745195637/7.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745195637/7.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745207775/8.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745207775/8.png)

2、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧松"接近开关"的一颗固定螺丝，使用十字螺丝刀拧松"导风罩"后方的一颗固定螺丝（在接近开关下方）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745509640/9.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745509640/9.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745520083/10.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745520083/10.png)

3、拔掉"喷嘴照明灯"的排线端口，向下取掉"导风罩"（在左侧风扇下方有卡扣设计，在角落位置更容易分离）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745564659/11.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745564659/11.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745573176/12.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745573176/12.png)

### 更换左侧模型散热风扇

1、使用十字螺丝刀拧松左侧"模型散热风扇"的三颗固定螺丝，拔掉"挤出转接板"中左侧模型散热风扇的端口，并取出左侧模型散热风扇。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745684587/13.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745684587/13.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745697116/14.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745697116/14.png)

2、将新的模型散热风扇的线端口插入挤出转接板的"FAN2"端口（端口有防呆设计，注意区分后插入），然后将模型散热风扇放到安装位置（风扇口朝下对准开口位置，螺丝孔对准螺丝柱子安装，不要压到连接线）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745749839/15.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745749839/15.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745758132/16.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745758132/16.png)

3、使用十字螺丝刀拧紧左侧"模型散热风扇"的三颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745795356/13.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745795356/13.png)

#### 更换右侧模型散热风扇

1、使用十字螺丝刀拧松右侧"模型散热风扇"的三颗固定螺丝，拔掉"挤出转接板"中右侧模型散热风扇的端口，并取出右侧模型散热风扇。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745842699/17.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745842699/17.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745852940/18.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745852940/18.png)

2、将新的模型散热风扇的线端口插入挤出转接板的"FAN2"端口（端口有防呆设计，注意区分后插入），然后将模型散热风扇放到安装位置（风扇口朝下对准开口位置，螺丝孔对准螺丝柱子安装，不要压到连接线）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745887064/19.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745887064/19.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745898253/20.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745898253/20.png)

3、使用十字螺丝刀拧紧右侧"模型散热风扇"的三颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745938132/17.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698745938132/17.png)

4、将"喷嘴照明灯"的排线穿过照明灯的开口，取出导风罩，将"喷嘴照明灯"的排线插入。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746148361/21.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746148361/21.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746456560/22.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746456560/22.png)

5、然后将喷嘴照明灯端口对准前方开口位置安装，向上轻轻按压导风罩，连接好卡扣。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746499446/23.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746499446/23.png)

6、使用十字螺丝刀拧紧"导风罩"底部的五颗固定螺丝（喷嘴照明灯旁边的两颗螺丝稍长一点），以及后方的一颗固定螺丝（在接近开关下方）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746552021/24.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746552021/24.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746557222/25.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746557222/25.png)

7、将"接近开关"放到安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧一颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746648327/9.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746648327/9.png)

### 3-安装打印头

1、安装打印头整体组件的前盖（有凹槽设计，滑入方式安装）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746716072/7.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746716072/7.png)

2、将打印头整体组件放到打印头前方安装位置，使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"打印头前盖"的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746818371/28.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746818371/28.png)
