[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746828690/29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746828690/29.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746837511/30.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746837511/30.png)

3、用手向两侧按压"牛角自锁端子"打开端口，然后将打印头排线端口插入端口（注意排线从顶部型材下方穿过）。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746940630/31%281%29.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746940630/31%281%29.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746960125/IMG_9261.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746960125/IMG_9261.jpg)

4、使用2.0mm内六角扳手拧紧"排线固定件"的两颗固定螺丝，以及打印头的两颗固定螺丝。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746997801/3.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698746997801/3.png)

5、取出风扇组件，对准螺丝孔安装位置，使用2.5mm内六角扳手拧紧后风扇组件的三颗固定螺丝（出风口朝下安装），插入风扇组件接口线端口。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698747036250/2.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698747036250/2.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698747048711/1.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698747048711/1.png)

6、开启打印机电源，在触摸屏上单击【设置-风扇】，打开打印头两侧的鼓风风扇，观察到两侧鼓风风扇正常旋转后，重新调平打印机就可以正常使用。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698747397893/36.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240725122954mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1698747397893/36.png)
# 无线网卡扩展教程

## 无线网卡类型选择

已经验证可行无线网卡如下，其他网卡不支持，不支持双频网卡

水星Mercury：MW150US免驱版本、

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1704175495946/5002.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1704175495946/5002.jpg)

普联TP-link： TL-WN725N免驱版本

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1704175520255/5001.jpg)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/61080e13-b61c-4b20-a5e8-053c8a8234b4/1704175520255/5001.jpg)

## 需要准备的工具和材料

● USB2.0  2.4G  无线网卡

● 容量为32GB以内的U盘

● 需要升级的固件包

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655585221/2.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655592169/image.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655592169/image.png)

容量为32GB以内的U盘

## 操作步骤

1、选择对应机器的固件包，双击打开"**ELEGOO_UPDATE_DIR**"名称的文件夹，找到并使用记事本打开“**wpa_supplicant-wlan0.conf**”文件。

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701684543611/3.png)

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701684551575/4.png)

2、在**ssid**的双引号中输入路由器的**WiFi账户**，**psk**的双引号中输入**WiFi密码**。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1702464755835/111.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1702464755835/111.png)

3、点击【**文件**】-【**保存**】。

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701684580640/6.png)

4、将"**ELEGOO_UPDATE_DIR**"名称的文件夹复制到U盘中（U盘需提前格式化清空）。

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701684595485/7.png)

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701684595485/7.png)

5、按照更新固件操作升级固件即可。

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655691597/8.png)
![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655698726/9.png)

![](https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655705126/10.png)

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655713522/11.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655713522/11.png)

6、  升级成功固件后，将无线网卡插入机器的USB端口重启机器，机器开机后会自动连接网络，在【**设置**】-【**信息**】界面即可查看IP网址。

[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341im_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655733156/12.png)](https://web.archive.org/web/20240714101341mp_/https://saas.bk-cdn.com/t/c45e7f57-b66a-4f11-895e-906d83ec6b4d/u/768b2550-d057-42ca-9898-14db7c7d10db/1701655733156/12.png)
